World Anecdotes 96

— Sea Guest

King Manuel II of Portugal. Manoel, since abdicating and leaving the country, has lived in England and France. He is an expert in horticulture and has written an important book discussing Portuguese literature.

Beggars in Birmingham, England, run their own newspaper called "The Abraham Man's News."

"The Abraham Man's News" is printed on a single sheet of mimeograph paper and costs one and a half pence. All the text is in the vernacular of the market.

The only countries in Europe that manufacture hand-cranked organs are Scotland and Belgium. In 1929, a centenary celebration was held. This was a very interesting commemorative ceremony.

According to Sir W. Scroder, a coroner in London, children between the ages of nine and thirteen are the best witnesses in court cases.

Greenland, in the Arctic region, is a very cold and desolate place in the far north. Recently, the United States used a wheelbarrow to transport wood there to build an auditorium, a parsonage, and a store. The wood has been pre-fabricated and only needs to be assembled to become houses.

The Trade of Humans 97

— Huang Yingdai

Using people as commodities for buying and selling. Those who engage in this profession, their cruelty is self-evident. In the past, there was the trade of black slaves in the Americas. Those who engaged in this business made considerable profits. It was not until Lincoln freed the black slaves and the Civil War was resolved that the sale of black slaves was no longer heard of. And with all the republics, we thought that black slaves would no longer be sold as human beings. Unexpectedly, in Africa, the slave system has been revived in recent years, and the trade of black slaves is thriving again.

But looking back at China, although there is no organization for trafficking in people, the business of selling people is quite developed, just like in Africa. There are also many people engaged in this business. Most of them are local ruffians and hooligans who have no means of making a living, so they engage in abducting and selling young boys and girls. It is said that young girls from the Suzhou area are most welcomed by overseas Chinese in Singapore. Generally, kidnappers abduct young girls and transport them to Singapore for sale. The profits are rare. It is said that in Singapore, there is a secret market for auctioning off young girls, and the business is quite developed. Therefore, there is an oversupply of young girls transported there.

Singapore is a necessary transit point for East-West traffic. The city is quite developed, and the society is quite complex. Therefore, there are more dark sides than anywhere else. Westerners often call it the "dark market" for this reason. In addition to the auction of young girls, there are also secret companies set up to sell children. Those who engage in this business have very flexible social skills and interact with wealthy people in the area. Therefore, all children can be sold. As for the source of the children, most of them are also abducted by kidnappers. In addition, poor people who are unable to support their children also entrust them to the company for sale.

In my hometown, those who engage in this trafficking of people are called "white ants" or "human head traffickers." Most of them are unemployed vagrants. Young girls with unstable wills are sometimes lured and sold by these people. In other cases, widows take the initiative to ask traffickers for help, or they are forced to marry by their in-laws, and traffickers act as underwriters to profit from it. These are particularly common. However, those who are sold are mostly young girls, so that they can be taken as wives or concubines. This kind of tragedy occurs from time to time and is also the misfortune of mankind.

Sunrise in the Mountains 98

— Chen Xiaocui

At night in the mountains, the smoke rises heavily, the crescent moon hangs like a carved bow at dawn. The cold clouds vast, transform into a sea, several peaks faintly immersed, like blue lotus. In this place where human footprints never reach, the dark color stretches far, connecting with the prehistoric wilderness. Looking down at the heavenly gate, a strip of striped carnelian. Suddenly, a single hair splits open the primordial chaos. Fu Xi tries his brush, Nüwa dies, there is a gap in the emotional sky that no one can sew. A beauty like a flower, separated by clouds, the tassel half-rolled, the lamp dimly red. Yi's bow flies and shoots arrows, the sound trails. The Xuanyuan mirror emerges from its box, the light is harmonious. Scales and armor of pure gold, painting the autumn waters, rolling up into the sky, all are fish and dragons. Looking down, the mortal world is still quiet, thousands and thousands of miles, no human traces. The red city glows with a carmine color, the trees all over the mountains are red maples. The floating clouds drift away with the distant wind. I will leave to find Chisongzi.

Record of Strange Events Regarding an Ancient Ginkgo Tree 99

— Li Biya

Kunshan and Jiading border each other. There is a stone beam called Datong Bridge. The area is named Datong Bridge. There is an ancient Jixian Temple next to the bridge. Most of it has been destroyed. The clay bodhisattvas are not sheltered from the wind and rain. The villagers want to rebuild it to preserve the ancient site. They are suffering from a lack of funds. That's all. Unexpectedly, there is now unexpected wealth flowing in, and the goal of rebuilding the ancient Jixian Temple will soon be achieved. It sounds very strange and inevitably involves superstition. However, this is what I witnessed and did not get from hearsay. I can tell the readers of Free Talk about it. In front of the mountain gate of the ancient Jixian Temple, there are two ancient ginkgo trees, lined up east and west. They are five or six spans in size. The elders say that they are ancient trees that are thousands of years old. Last month, one of the western trees suddenly caught fire. The tree was hollow. The fire flew out from the hollow. There was a defense team nearby. They bravely came to rescue. It took five or six hours to extinguish it. Where the fire flew out, a large branch broke off. It was several feet long and the size of a hug. As for the cause of the fire, opinions differ. Some say that a monk threw the remaining incense into the hollow of the tree roots. Some say that a passerby rested, leaning against the tree roots, and the remaining incense smoke was left in the root hole. Decayed leaves accumulated in the hole, causing it to ignite. The latter saying is accidental and not surprising. The former saying seems to have an effect. Of those who believe the former saying now, more than ninety out of a hundred. Several days after the ancient ginkgo tree was destroyed by the fire, someone suddenly came from Zhenru, Nanchang to peel the bark of the ancient ginkgo tree that had been destroyed. It is said that someone said that this is a miraculous elixir that can cure all diseases. The next day, more people came. The local people, to prevent the ancient trees from not being burned to death by the fire, died from peeling the bark. So they surrounded it with bamboo fences, and because they begged to take the elixir, they broke off a large branch, analyzed it, and gave it to the comers. After a day or two, more and more people came. The local people said that they could take this opportunity to build the ancient Jixian Temple to preserve the ancient site. So the yellow book was established, and the donors were numerous. There is a general situation of the minister's door being like a market. It is said that since the establishment of the yellow book, three copies have been changed. The current payment has accumulated about two or three hundred silver dollars. There are also this number of people who have donated but have not yet paid. There are also wealthy people who are willing to donate hundreds of tube tiles and tens of thousands of wall bricks, enthusiastically transporting them. They all said that even if they take one or two leaves of the ancient ginkgo tree and decoct them, the disease will be cured immediately. Therefore, the payment of wishes is rapid. At first, I did not believe it. I went to watch with a friend and exclaimed in amazement. My friend said to me, "The ancient ginkgo tree has the heart to save the world and is willing to sacrifice itself to avoid the suffering of the sick. It is touching." I responded, "Our people have suffered a lot. Who wouldn't be willing to burn incense and bow down to those who can sacrifice themselves to save them? It is a pity that those who have the heart to save the world do not have the great power of the ancient ginkgo tree. Those who have the great power similar to the ancient ginkgo tree have no heart to save the world. Where can our people go to beg for elixir?"

Miscellaneous Talks on Loquats 100

— Zheng Yimei

"The loquat is slightly yellow, still bearing a hint of sourness." This is a line from Su Changgong's poem. Loquat is another name for loquat. The "Group of Fragrances" says that loquats sprout in autumn, flower in winter, bear fruit in spring, and ripen in summer, possessing the energy of all four seasons. No other fruit can compare. It is indeed a precious fruit. In this sweltering weather, with fragrant loquats in a green basket, I casually write this essay, and I cannot help but feel my saliva dripping.

It is said that Scholar Zhu Zha of Xiushui was close friends with a certain Taoist priest. There were two loquat trees in the Taoist temple. During hot weather, he often saw the loquats being harvested. None of them had seeds. Zhu Zha asked the reason. The Taoist priest replied that they were immortal seeds. Zhu Zha did not believe it. He knew that the Taoist priest loved steamed pork. One day, he invited him over and ordered a servant to buy a pig's shoulder. He purposely showed it to the Taoist priest, and before long, it was served as a dish. It was thoroughly cooked, fatty, and delicious. The Taoist priest ate his fill. Then he asked Zhu Zha about the method of quick transformation. Zhu Zha said, "I happen to have a small trick, which I would like to exchange for the loquat seed." The Taoist priest whispered, "It's nothing. Just pluck out the central stamen when it first blooms." Zhu Zha said, "Then my dish is nothing special either. It was what I had prepared beforehand." They both clapped their hands and laughed. Loquats without seeds are called "Jiaozi" and are found in Guangzhou, according to the "Guang Zhi."

Once, in Li Xiushan's secretariat, there was a secretary who had a concubine named "Red Loquat." The concubine was good at playing the pipa and loved to eat loquats, hence the name. Gan Zhi wrote the "Elegy of the Pipa's Shadow" for Red Loquat, depicting her life story with utmost sorrow and captivating beauty. It was widely recited at the time.

Loquat leaves are as big as donkey ears. Cantonese people call them "Worry-Free Fans." Boiling them for drinking can cure coughs. However, there is a fuzzy yellow down on the back, which should be brushed off. Otherwise, it will not only be useless but also harmful. Therefore, sick people often buy ready-made loquat leaf dew to replace it.

My Suzhou Dongting Mountain is famous for producing loquats. There are red sand and white sand varieties. White sand is better. There is also a small, flat variety called "Water Chestnut Seed," which is even more superior.

"The wind and dew fill the sky, the loquats are ripe, I bring them home to offer to my loving mother, to taste as she pleases." This is a line from Chen Ji's poem. Reading it, one cannot help but feel filial piety arise spontaneously. There are also Bai Juyi's poem, "On the side of Huai Mountain, the shadow of the Chu River, in May, the loquats fill the forest," and Lu You's poem, "The branches are not afraid of the wind shaking them down, the tree only worries about the birds pecking them away," all of which add to the luster of loquats.

Loquat. Seeds sprout directly. Wait for them to grow before transplanting. In the third month of spring, graft them with other woody plants. Cover them with ashes. The branches and leaves dance, and they do not wither in the frost, hence the name "Late Verdant Loquat."

Loquat jelly is a refined food. The method is to peel and pit the loquats, cut them into thin slices, add an appropriate amount of water, and simmer them over a low fire until they are soft and mushy. Strain the juice, mix it with powdered sugar, place it in a candied fruit jar, simmer for a few minutes to melt the sugar, then heat it to a boil. Pour it into a glass basin, seal it, and immerse it in cold water for about half an hour. It will become a clear jelly.

Cultural Movements That the Capital Should Undertake in the Future (Part 1) 101

— Wang Yachen

The term "exhibition" has only been around for fifteen years in our country. Before that, there was only the term "Sai Zeng" (a type of folk performance). It first evolved from the masses. People like us who study art often hold exhibitions. In the last ten years, there have been international, group, and private art movements of various kinds. At least it has awakened the public to the concept of "exhibition." In the spring of the 18th year (of the Republic), Shanghai held a National Art Exhibition, sponsored by the Ministry of Education. And the First Art Exhibition recently opened in the capital is even more worthy of our attention. Because the venue is in the capital. (Exhibitions held by the state are held in the capital). I have two points about the significance of the capital hosting art exhibitions to promote cultural undertakings that I want to state first. All public exhibitions related to cultural movements, especially those sponsored by national educational institutions, must have a permanent organization. It is definitely not enough to hold one occasionally and then let it pass. It must be held every year within a prescribed time. If you just think about holding it, and stop if there is no funding or you are afraid of trouble, the effect is minimal. There must be a first session, a second session, and so on indefinitely. From the simplicity of the first session to gradual perfection. From the crudeness of the works in the first session to gradual refinement. This all needs to be corrected through careful management. This is my first hope.

All exhibitions held by national educational institutions must have rewards after review. The improvement of public art and the efforts of various artists all depend on the government agencies having corresponding rewards. After the award methods are established, the quality of the exhibits will increase year by year. On the one hand, it will make various artists bury themselves in their work, and on the other hand, it will produce the essence of national art. This is my second hope.

In addition to the above two hopes, what is even more needed after the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, thinking from this exhibition, is the movement to prepare for the Capital Art Museum. And I hope that everyone will support the art museum movement, to add glory to the Chinese nation, to promote and carry forward our country's culture for thousands of years, to be a cultural leader in the capital after the success of the revolution, and for the appearance of the emerging capital, there must be an art museum organization. In various European countries I have traveled to, not to mention that cities have art museums and museum facilities, even a small town has a small-scale embellishment. Last winter, when I returned to China from Europe, I felt the necessity of organizing an art museum. I discussed it with Mr. Li Shizeng and Cai Zimin in Shanghai, and Mr. Li agreed. First, an art exhibition hall was established in Shanghai. It is currently under construction and will be completed in two months. But I think it is even more necessary to establish an art museum in Nanjing than in Shanghai. Because the capital is the center of the country, where people look, and especially the cultural symbol of a country must be tasted in art. Now there are foreigners stepping on my land and coming to my capital. If they ask where the art museum is, we have nothing to answer. It is truly regrettable. Therefore, we must have a movement to organize an art museum.

Rotary Club of Novels

Three Eras (8) 102

— Zhang Henshui

He shrugged his shoulders as he said this. The crow's feet at the corners of his eyes all moved, showing his pride. He continued, "Tell me, first, second, and third-class prostitutes, which one can't you go to? If you go and pick a girl, that's the group, right? Drinking fragrant tea and smoking cigarettes to your heart's content. They wouldn't dare take your money. Those little girls in the top-class groups, you've seen them on the road. Would they even give you a proper look? But once you become a soldier, they have to serve you. The benefits of being a soldier are endless. Don't be afraid of fighting. If there's no war, where do soldiers go to make a name for themselves? Haven't you heard? Liu Bei sold straw sandals, Zhang Fei sold meat, and Lord Guan even drove a cart. Didn't they all end up as brothers as ruler and subjects because of fighting? Xue Rengui was named Prince of Pingliao. Anyone who's seen the play knows he went to join the army as a beggar, right? A hero isn't afraid of a humble beginning. It all depends on what you do. Our division commander started as a common soldier. Now look at his power! Mansions, cars, concubines! Is there anything he doesn't have? Where else can you go to win merit if not in war? A real man shouldn't be afraid of death. From the day a person is born, the King of Hell has already determined their lifespan. If it's not time to die, you won't die. If it is, you can't escape. As the saying goes, 'What is destined cannot be avoided. The country is always conquered by fighting.' Waiting for free food to fall into your mouth? That's never going to happen. If you want to make a name for yourselves, come join the army with me. You can't go wrong. If you're doing petty business, you'll do petty business your whole life. If you're pulling rickshaws, you'll pull rickshaws your whole life. In this colorful world, if you don't get your share of anything, you've come for nothing. I've finished talking. Are there any volunteers?" As soon as he said this, two people walked out of the crowd and said, "Commander, I'll go!" The soldier smiled and said, "Good for you for being so sensible. Who else?" As he spoke, he swept his gaze over the crowd like a machine gun, landing on Zhang Xiaosan. Zhang Xiaosan said, "Okay, I'll go too." As he spoke, he walked in front of the soldier, rubbing his hands together and looking around, as if he didn't know what to do. The soldier said, "You sit with them first. We'll leave together in a while." So Zhang Xiaosan joined the group of people listening to the speech. The soldier continued his speech with a smile. No one else knew how happy he was in his heart. Because if everyone was so eager to join the army, he could easily recruit a platoon in half a day. According to the rules of his camp, he could at least become a platoon leader.

Art World

The Hurricane 120

Will Publish as a Separate Volume

Mr. Gu Jianchen's newly written three-act play, "The Hurricane," has reportedly already been rehearsed at the Wuxi Educational Institute. We read Mr. Tianniu's article, "Presenting 'The Hurricane' to the Modern Theatrical World," in the Shenbao on the 19th of this month, and learned that the play depicts the conflict between the Chinese and Japanese nations with Manchuria and Mongolia as the backdrop, using a Korean woman as the main thread of the entire play. In the play, the young man Yang Zhiqin gathers comrades to implement a plan to develop Manchuria and Mongolia, but it is sabotaged by the Japanese. The map and plan are lost, and Yang Zhiqin suffers an unjust accusation. He is not only spurned by the people, but his fiancée also cancels their engagement. Rumors outside accuse him of being lured by the Japanese and he is labeled a traitor. Unable to clear his name, he becomes ill. Fortunately, Ono Umeko, who believes herself to be Japanese, realizes that she is actually a Korean woman and confesses in front of the Chinese, returning the stolen map and plan. However, the poor young man Yang Zhiqin has already gone mad and committed suicide. Later, the Korean woman is also killed by the Japanese. When we see such a plot, how moving it is! We hope that this script will be published soon so that we can read it first. Moreover, at a time when the school play movement is booming and there is a shortage of scripts, this kind of script is worth adopting for performance. It is now said that Mr. Gu has sent the original manuscript to the Vanguard Weekly, and the magazine will publish it in issues 45, 46, 47, and 48, and will combine these issues of the Weekly into a separate volume, completely publishing Mr. Gu's script, equivalent to a separate edition of "The Hurricane," which will be published soon. The general distributor is Daguang Bookstore, Ximenfang Xielu.

After Viewing Mr. Suzuki's Oil Painting Exhibition 121

— Chen Baoyi

The "Oil Painting Exhibition of Mr. Ryozo Suzuki," held at the Japanese Club a few days ago (May 29th and 30th), was one of the most outstanding Japanese Western-style painting exhibitions recently held.

I had heard Mr. Ryozo Suzuki's name before, but this was the first time I saw his work.

There were over fifty works on display, mostly landscapes, the fruits of his sketching trip to China this time. There were also several portraits.

There are many excellent works among the exhibits... His style is a realism that does not fall into the trap of sweetness... Although it exudes a delicate and harmonious coordination, it has a robust and clear expression... The picture plane is handled with composure, and one type is shrouded in a silver-gray harmony... Another type has light and delicate mass (volume of color), interspersed with gentle, delicate line drawing... These are lines cleverly used according to what he is trying to express.

As for the works, in addition to what seem to be the artist's prized pieces... "The Shade of the Willow," "Girl," "Autumn Moon on the Calm Lake" (No. 1), "Small Scene on the Lake Shore," etc., there are many other excellent works. To briefly mention a few, for example:

"West Lake Pleasure Boat" (Sketch, about 3 hao in size), depicting a portion of the lake surface... The lake surface is a somber lead color, with a yacht with a white awning floating among the gentle ripples, a quiet and lovely small piece.

"Spring Rain on West Lake" (25 hao in size) is a painting depicted with a high degree of detail. On the left side of the foreground is part of a white wall. The old trees and shrubs in front and below the mountain are depicted in gentle and quiet bright and dark greens. The lake water, sky, and the entire harmony drift in a hazy light silver-gray.

"Afternoon Glare" is a painting depicting a clear and dark green water surface, and buildings and trees in the foreground depicted in somber warm colors, beautifully harmonized... In colors that are not particularly bright, it gives one a refreshing sense of the warm sunshine of the afternoon bathing the entire scene.

"Autumn Moon on the Calm Lake" (No. 2) (painting about 30 hao in size)... This uses architecture as its theme, depicted in somber colors, and is very capable of expressing the beauty and interest of our country's ancient architecture. In terms of its depiction, it is also seen to be expressed extremely appropriately, and although realistic, it does not fall into triviality.

The large "House by the Pond" primarily depicts a section of a house, a long corridor, and trees (two women in red and blue clothing stand in the shade of the corridor). Shade and light intersect gently across the entire picture, and the colors, though bright, have a certain solidity, beautifully expressing the sentiment of early summer.

"Early Summer on Tianping Mountain" (large)... The trees and mountain scenery are harmonized in color. In particular, the distant high mountains, with their craggy rocks, are expressed lightly in a pale purple tinged with ocher and pale green.

"Early Summer Path" is also a painting that is very capable of expressing the sentiments of an early summer garden. The brushwork is brisk and clear, and the colors of the trees, walls, and stone paths in the distance and near make a beautiful harmony.

"Liuyuan Garden" depicts a somber, brownish-green pond, with an old tree stretching obliquely over the water surface, and the white reflection of the buildings opposite... The overall tone is somber and elegant, filled with the charm of an ancient garden.

"New Greenery at the Humble Administrator's Garden" (large)... takes the architecture in the garden as its theme... The beauty of the architecture is wonderfully embellished amidst the contrasting light and shade of the vibrant foliage.

"Beside Fangyuan Garden"... depicts a cow in front of a white wall and two old trees with light brushstrokes. The colors are light, simple, and contain a poetic feeling in an ancient style.

In addition, there is also "Kaiyuan Temple Road" with its pale blue sky, yellow walls, and dark road... "House by the Water," which is mainly black... "Releasing Fish Garden," with its somber brownish-green water surface and buildings and pavilions in the distance and near, etc., are all deeply evocative.

As for the depiction of figures, I consider the half-length portrait of a woman wearing black clothes against a silver-gray background... the half-length portrait of a man wearing gray clothes against a black background, "Portrait of Mr. I"... and the village girl "Country Girl," painted in black tones against a light ocher background, to be the best.

Originally, Mr. Suzuki was a craftsman. In 1922, he graduated from Jikei University School of Medicine. He helped his father in his business with his brother and ran the Mito Shimoichi Hospital. However, on the one hand, he loved painting deeply since childhood and was taught by the late talented painter Mr. Nakamura... Since the spring of 1923, when his work was exhibited at the "Art Exhibition of the Peace Exposition," his name has been known in the art world. His passion for art finally triumphed over the will of his profession, and he was encouraged by various forces, and then resolutely gave up his profession and devoted himself to the refinement of the art of painting. He went to France in 1928 to study for three years, and returned to China last December. Last autumn, his work was exhibited at the "Imperial Art Exhibition" and was nominated for "Special Selection." Some of his works have been purchased and collected by famous people... Mr. Suzuki, who shifted from medicine to art, and is grasping solid strength to open up his artistic realm, is indeed a unique figure in the current Japanese Western-style painting world... I feel delighted by his attitude of pursuing his creative work with a pure love for art, and I also find it admirable.

Shanghai Market

Market News 122

Sincere Company announces: Our second-floor silk and satin department has newly arrived printed Georgette, Indian silk, gold-threaded and silver-flowered Zosan silk, and other high-quality summer clothing materials. The novelty of the designs and the vibrancy of the colors are said to be unseen in Shanghai.

Good Morning Friends Society announces: Zhang Zhenyuan's self-created "Good Morning Stationery," with thousands of drawing plates, is the champion of the stationery industry. Using his novelist background to create industry, people often compare him to Tianxu Wo Sheng's invincible "Tooth Powder." Our main store is located at Beijing Road, Lunjibridge, and the south store is at Dou City Street. All published and bound "Good Morning Stationery," such as the West Lake Scenery series, New Makeup series, Collection series, Satirical Painting series, and Special Painting series, have long been bestsellers. Recently, we have released a new "Good Morning Stationery" landscape painting series, each containing one hundred sheets, selected from twenty vertical landscape paintings by Gao Henian, printed in five colors, with printed hidden grids, and eight lines. The domestic Yun Dui paper is priced at four corners per book, Yu Zhu paper at three corners and a half per book, and Lian Shi paper at three corners. Our society also accepts custom printing of stationery envelopes and other printed materials. Please enclose a postal note when requesting stationery samples.

Yan Hua Lou Restaurant, located west of the "Immortal World" on the Fourth Avenue, announces: Our restaurant has been creating Cantonese cuisine for over twenty years, with exquisite cooking techniques, refined seasoning, and affordable prices, which have always been praised by all sectors of society. Therefore, business is booming. The owner of the restaurant, recognizing that summer has arrived and that the Fourth Avenue area is the most bustling place, and that there is still a lack of fine ice parlors, has specially opened the downstairs as an ice parlor for the convenience of all. The decor is elegant, clean, and hygienic, selling Beauty Brand ice cream, various shaved ice, and soda, all fully stocked, wholesale and retail. The prices are especially favorable. Qing Yi Se Restaurant at the intersection of Third Avenue and Zhejiang Road, at the same time, various iced drinks are also available.

Youth Corner

After Returning 123

— Jun

Drunk, not knowing where to go, I sleep hazily in the shadow of the green pines—

These are the last two lines of a verse that Huang, who had once disappeared and recently returned from afar, showed us at the New Asia welcome party the day before yesterday. He drew it at a temple in Huishan, Wuxi. Because this event left such a deep impression on me, I can't forget it, especially these two meaningful lines of verse.

Huang's disappearance this time was really too abrupt. He left without a word. Even his closest friend, Mo, didn't know anything about it beforehand. Regarding his unusual action, I only know that in the moment before he left, he hurriedly handed a small and very scribbled note to his sister, Ying, who had just finished class. Then, the hearts of all of Huang's friends were stirred by this note, because it reported to us an abrupt fact. It was scribbled with a few lines of pencil writing:

"Classmate Wenying, now I report to you a piece of news about me, whether it is fortunate or unfortunate. That is, I have decided to leave from now on. Life is originally vast and indistinct, and because of this, vagueness is life. Love can save people, but it can also kill people, because it is ultimately a stage in the vast and indistinct journey of life. Now I want to thoroughly complete this vague task of my life. In fact, aren't all things in the universe like this? Because you know more about everything about me, I'm telling you this. I don't want to say more here. Please don't worry about me, and please forward this to other friends. Goodbye, Huang XX, X Month X Day."

So, because of the report in this note, all of us friends who cared about Huang were very busy doing the work of finding and inquiring about Huang. Among them, those who felt particularly sad and miserable were, of course, Miss Zhang and Shen, who loved Huang in the local area. But what was the result? We were all filled with disappointment. Huang ultimately disappeared like a wild goose into the dark sky, a stone sinking into the sea. We couldn't get any news or trace of him. We could only helplessly pray for good news to descend from heaven in a state of anxiety and disappointment.

After nearly ten days of such waiting, suddenly, one afternoon, Mo came to our residence with a look of joy that he rarely had. He came to report to us the news that Huang had returned! This, you can imagine, how happy and comforted we were. So we all rushed to Huang's house and invited him to New Asia for a snack, to have a hearty reunion after the separation. And at the same time, we also got to see the heroines in this tragicomedy, Miss Zhang and Shen.

The problems that young people feel most distressed about now are, of course, the problems of career and love. Because these two problems cannot be solved, young people often take risks and stage many tragedies, but what is the result? They still can't be solved. This is really a problem that has a huge impact on the life of society and the country and urgently needs to be solved. This time, our Huang's departure was also because he felt that his love problem could not be solved. But what made Huang different from others was that he didn't leave because of a broken heart. He left because he was under attack from two women who were very passionate about him. Really, Miss Zhang and Miss Shen were both very worthy of being loved. So how can you blame Huang for being at a loss and not knowing what to do? But according to Huang himself, he was very much in love with Shen, even though he had loved Zhang before, and Zhang still loves him, forgetting herself, and it is generally recognized by the society that he and Zhang are a future couple, but he always only loves Shen. This is really an unsolvable case.

When we arrived at New Asia, we happily ate the dishes while we freely discussed everything that had happened since our separation. In these conversations, we all felt a new vitality dancing in our heads. Until almost halfway through the drinking, Huang stood up excitedly, holding a glass filled to the brim with wine. With a very firm yet very desolate expression, he said the following words to us:

"My friends, come on, let's all drain this full glass. Today is the beginning of our new life, and it is also the beginning of your new life. Everything in the past has become a thing of the past. Let's just let it pass. But let's not let the coming future slip away lightly before our eyes. We must firmly grasp it. Pessimism, negativity, decadence, world-weariness, these are only found in the mouths of people who are useless. I am now awake. I know these are not very worthwhile. These are not the solutions we are seeking. These are just a trap of self-indulgence. Now, friends, we should all strive to pursue the acquisition of our light, and then we can proceed to solve other problems. This is the right way. Friends, let's all work together!"

Originally, everyone's heart was very peaceful and happy, but after listening to his firm tone and the words that would touch our hearts, our hearts were gradually assimilated by him. We only felt that on the leaves of our hearts, a taste suddenly floated up that we couldn't distinguish as sweet, sour, bitter, or spicy. It was truly a unique taste in our hearts. After we finished listening to his words, no one said anything, just looked at each other and smiled knowingly, and drank the full cup very painfully. Ah, this situation, it is impossible to describe and express with clumsy words and languages. Only those who are personally present can understand it.

On the way back, I only hoped for and worried about the friend after returning, Huang, the friend of new life.

Regulations for Youth Corner Contributions 124

(1) The content of the articles should be about the discussion of youth issues, news from domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, and notes, and the style is not limited.

(2) The pictures should be limited to those related to youth issues.

(3) The photos should be qualified if they show youth life (such as sports, travel, sightseeing, drama performance, assembly, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements. Individuals and groups are welcome. Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.
